// Generic functions






38



template <typename T, size_t N>






39



KFR_SINTRIN vec<T, N> saturated_signed_add(const vec<T, N>& a, const vec<T, N>& b)






40



{






41



    using UT               = utype<T>;






42



    constexpr size_t shift = typebits<UT>::bits - 1;






43



    vec<UT, N> aa        = bitcast<UT>(a);








inline

                           
 kfr::vec<unsigned int, 4ul> kfr::bitcast<unsigned int, int, 4ul, 4ul>(kfr::vec<int, 4ul> const&) should always be inlined (cost=always) 		
kfr::vec kfr::intrinsics::saturated_signed_add(kfr::vec const&, kfr::vec const&)







inline

                           
 kfr::vec<unsigned int, 4ul> kfr::bitcast<unsigned int, int, 4ul, 4ul>(kfr::vec<int, 4ul> const&) inlined into kfr::vec<int, 4ul> kfr::intrinsics::saturated_signed_add<int, 4ul>(kfr::vec<int, 4ul> const&, kfr::vec<int, 4ul> const&) 		
kfr::vec kfr::intrinsics::saturated_signed_add(kfr::vec const&, kfr::vec const&)







inline

                           
 kfr::vec<unsigned long, 2ul> kfr::bitcast<unsigned long, long, 2ul, 2ul>(kfr::vec<long, 2ul> const&) should always be inlined (cost=always) 		
kfr::vec kfr::intrinsics::saturated_signed_add(kfr::vec const&, kfr::vec const&)







inline

                           
 kfr::vec<unsigned long, 2ul> kfr::bitcast<unsigned long, long, 2ul, 2ul>(kfr::vec<long, 2ul> const&) inlined into kfr::vec<long, 2ul> kfr::intrinsics::saturated_signed_add<long, 2ul>(kfr::vec<long, 2ul> const&, kfr::vec<long, 2ul> const&) 		
kfr::vec kfr::intrinsics::saturated_signed_add(kfr::vec const&, kfr::vec const&)





44



    vec<UT, N> bb        = bitcast<UT>(b);








inline

                           
 kfr::vec<unsigned int, 4ul> kfr::bitcast<unsigned int, int, 4ul, 4ul>(kfr::vec<int, 4ul> const&) should always be inlined (cost=always)

kfr::vec kfr::intrinsics::saturated_signed_add(kfr::vec const&, kfr::vec const&)





45



    const vec<UT, N> sum = aa + bb;








inline

                              
 kfr::operator+(kfr::vec<unsigned int, 4ul> const&, kfr::vec<unsigned int, 4ul> const&) can be inlined into kfr::vec<int, 4ul> kfr::intrinsics::saturated_signed_add<int, 4ul>(kfr::vec<int, 4ul> const&, kfr::vec<int, 4ul> const&) with cost=-35 (threshold=562)

    aa = (aa >> shift) + static_cast<UT>(std::numeric_limits<T>::max());

47









48



    return select(bitcast<T>((aa ^ bb) | ~(bb ^ sum)) >= 0, a, bitcast<T>(sum));

50



template <typename T, size_t N>






51



KFR_SINTRIN vec<T, N> saturated_signed_sub(const vec<T, N>& a, const vec<T, N>& b)






52



{






53



    using UT               = utype<T>;






54



    constexpr size_t shift = typebits<UT>::bits - 1;






55



    vec<UT, N> aa         = bitcast<UT>(a);








inline

                            
 kfr::vec<unsigned int, 4ul> kfr::bitcast<unsigned int, int, 4ul, 4ul>(kfr::vec<int, 4ul> const&) should always be inlined (cost=always) 		
kfr::vec kfr::intrinsics::saturated_signed_sub(kfr::vec const&, kfr::vec const&)

170



template <typename E1, typename E2, KFR_ENABLE_IF(is_input_expressions<E1, E2>::value)>






171



KFR_INTRIN internal::expression_function<fn::satadd, E1, E2> satadd(E1&& x, E2&& y)






172



{






173



    return { fn::satadd(), std::forward<E1>(x), std::forward<E2>(y) };






174



}

183



template <typename E1, typename E2, KFR_ENABLE_IF(is_input_expressions<E1, E2>::value)>






184



KFR_INTRIN internal::expression_function<fn::satsub, E1, E2> satsub(E1&& x, E2&& y)






185



{






186



    return { fn::satsub(), std::forward<E1>(x), std::forward<E2>(y) };






187



}
